\]\]><!\[CDATA\[ Senior Manager, Radio System Engineering (32647) \]\]>As the Senior Manager of Radio System Engineering, you will lead all technical aspects of radio system architecture, including air interface definition, concept of operations, functional specifications, and physical implementation of RF functions.

* * *

**Main Responsibilities:**

- Provide expert-level leadership in RF system development, including trade-offs involving ACP, PAR, out-of-band emissions, pass-band ripple, group delay, and more.

- Support the finalization of radio system implementation involving agile multi-beam phased array antennas and beam hopping technology.

- Define operational concepts for all phases of the system lifecycle such as user terminal commissioning, network entry, satellite handovers, time synchronization, and adaptive coding and modulation (ACM).

- Act as the principal architect for defining air interfaces between user terminals, ground infrastructure, and satellite payloads.

- Collaborate with RF, antenna, system, and terminal engineers to partition functionality between hardware and software components.

- Provide input to the system modeling team on design assumptions and strategies for modeling link performance, accounting for impairments across system components.

- Work closely with the Verification and Test team to ensure thorough validation of requirements and system performance.

- Participate in relevant industry standards forums (e.g., DVB) and provide strategic recommendations to align internal systems with evolving standards.

\]\]><!\[CDATA\[ Systems Configuration Identification Specialist (32646) \]\]>**Main Responsibilities:**

**Configuration Identification**

- Maintain an inventory of system assets (hardware).

- Control and document system, hardware, and software configurations, including both "as-designed" and "as-built" baselines.


**Software Configuration Management – Release Monitoring**

- Collaborate with technical teams and project management to define roles and responsibilities for configuration and release management.

- Work with development, test environment, and verification teams to define and document processes for managing software releases.

- For each release, verify required documentation is complete, approved, and captured, and ensure release packages are created in accordance with established procedures.

- Confirm that pending or outstanding changes do not impact planned test or release activities.

- Support development, lab, and test teams to ensure timely and accurate release execution.

- Assist with impact assessments and update the CI Tree and related configuration documentation to reflect approved changes.

- Support preparation and execution of configuration item status accounting and configuration audits.

- Provide subject matter expertise on configuration management (CM) processes, standards, and systems.

- Contribute to requirements management and traceability process documentation and improvement.

- Develop training materials for CM identification, software/release management, and general CM procedures.

- Participate in continuous improvement initiatives to enhance CM process efficiency, reliability, and cost-effectiveness.


**Document and Library Management Support**

- Initiate updates to documentation based on approved change requests.

- Collaborate with document management personnel to track and complete implementation of documentation updates.

- Ensure all released documents are logged, captured, and statused in the document management system.

- Act as backup support for document management responsibilities when needed.

- Bachelor’s or college degree in engineering, science, or a related field (or equivalent combination of education and experience).

- 3–6 years of experience in an engineering design environment working with systems, hardware, software, and test teams.

- 2+ years of experience in configuration and/or data management.

- 2+ years of experience in release management.

- Formal training, certification, or experience with CM standards (e.g., CM2, ANSI-EIA 649, ISO 10007).

- Experience with software configuration management tools and processes.

- Collaborative, team-oriented, and self-driven.

The contractor will support global SEO operations and partner with market teams to enhance visibility, discoverability, and performance across digital properties.<br> <br> Duration: July – December 2025, with potential extension<br> Location: Grand Rapids, MI (Onsite)<br> Reports to: Global SEO Lead<br> <br> Key Responsibilities<br> <br> Operational SEO Execution<br> • Conduct keyword research to support market-level needs and content planning.<br> • Perform technical SEO audits using tools like Ahrefs and Google Search Console.<br> • Support content optimization efforts, including metadata, on-page structure, and internal linking.<br> • Compile and deliver monthly SEO performance reports using platforms such as Ahrefs, Heap, and GSC.<br> • Troubleshoot SEO issues reported by markets and provide actionable solutions.<br> • Leverage AI tools and approaches to generate recommendations for content optimization, keyword discovery, link-building, and landing page refinement.<br> • Integrate AI-enabled tools to automate repetitive SEO tasks and improve execution speed and scalability.<br> <br> SEO Training and Enablement<br> • Assist in delivering SEO onboarding sessions and office hours for market teams.<br> • Help maintain and update SEO playbooks, best practices, and documentation on SharePoint.<br> • Create or revise modular self-serve resources to enable independent market optimization.<br> • Support the creation and management of a centralized SharePoint hub for training.<br> <br> Performance Monitoring and Insights<br> • Support organic search sentiment analysis and reputation tracking.<br> • Monitor and extract insights from dashboards (Heap, Ahrefs) to identify trends and risks.<br> • Assist in evaluating SEO impact for major product launches and post-launch performance reviews.<br> • Apply AI-powered tools to surface deeper insights from large-scale performance data.<br> <br> Collaboration and Coordination<br> • Work cross-functionally with content, analytics, and technical teams to integrate SEO best practices.<br> • Participate in global team meetings or planning sessions to ensure SEO considerations are included.<br> • Escalate technical SEO issues or strategic risks to the Global SEO Lead.<br> <br> Tool and Vendor Support<br> • Assist with user access management, licensing coordination, and onboarding for SEO tools.<br> • Support evaluations of SEO tool usage and effectiveness.<br> • Coordinate with vendors to troubleshoot issues or implement platform improvements.<br> <br> ?<br> <br> Qualifications<br> • 5+ years of experience in digital marketing and hands-on SEO in global or multi-market settings.<br> • Proficiency with SEO tools like Heap, Ahrefs, Google Search Console, and Lumar (or equivalent).<br> • Strong analytical skills; able to turn performance data into clear, actionable insights.<br> • Excellent writing and editing skills, with an understanding of search-optimized content.<br> • Demonstrated experience creating or reviewing metadata, headers, and on-page copy for SEO.<br> • Familiarity with CMS platforms and technical SEO concepts (indexing, crawling, Core Web Vitals).<br> • Strong understanding of how AI can be applied to SEO (e.g., prompt engineering, content summarization, automated content audits, keyword clustering).<br> • Experience working with cross-functional teams across content, marketing, and tech.<br> • Ability to work independently, manage multiple priorities, and adapt in a fast-paced environment.<br> </td> </tr> <!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Title: </strong>Cyber Posture Management Analyst</p> <p><strong>Type: </strong>Direct Hire</p> <p><strong>Location: </strong>Lansing, Michigan</p> <p>Clover Consulting (a Myticas Co.) has a large, direct client seeking a skilled Cyber Posture Mgmt. Analyst I to join the team as part of their Information Security & Privacy team. This position provides security analysis for the company's Identity and Access Management (IAM) Operation's program. This role requires knowledge across multiple platforms, applications, processes, and procedures to enable access management of business initiatives across the enterprise.</p> <p><strong><u>Essential Responsibilities</u></strong></p> <ul> <li>Familiar with identity and access management, with a focus on Privileged Access Management (PAM), Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA), and Identity Governance and Administration (IGA). <li>Knowledge of scripting languages (e.g., PowerShell, Python) for automation and customization of IAM solutions. <li>Understanding of identity protocols and technologies: OpenID Connect (OIDC,) OAuth, SAML, AD-Fed, API Gateways, SCIM, and platforms such as, Sailpoint, CyberArk, and MS Entra. <li>Knowledge of identity & access management vulnerabilities, threats and mitigations. <li>Ability to determine how a security system works (including its resilience and dependability capabilities) and how changes in conditions, operations, or the environment will affect these outcomes. <li>Familiar with modern software life cycle development and automated cloud infrastructure deployment. <li>Understanding of network architecture, operating systems, and security protocols. <li>Ability to work independently and collaboratively in a fast-paced environment. <li>Supports initiatives and projects that will improve the organization’s cyber posture. <li>Excellent analytical and problem-solving skills. <li>Strong communication and interpersonal skills. <li>Understanding of security controls, risk management, and regulatory compliance (NIST CSF/SOX/GDPR/etc.). <li>Extended hours, including on-call may be required. </ul> <p><strong><u>Knowledge, Skills and Abilities</u></strong></p> <ul> <li>Ability to receive and incorporate feedback. <li>Strong verbal and written communication skills. <li>Strong attention to detail. <li>Strong interpersonal, analytical, and problem-solving skills. <li>Flexibility in day-to-day work. <li>Ability to learn the company’s supported systems and their interfaces with other systems. <li>Strong knowledge of Microsoft software applications. <li>Ability to communicate technical concepts in an understandable fashion. <li>Ability to prioritize multiple tasks and execute efficiently and effectively while demonstrating a clear sense of urgency when appropriate. <li>Excellent customer service focus and skills. <li>Ability to collaborate effectively in a team environment to achieve desired results. <li>Scripting knowledge preferred. </ul> <p><strong><u>Qualifications</u></strong></p> <ul> <li>Bachelor's Degree or equivalent experience and/or education required. <li>1+ years knowledge of financial products, regulatory requirements, and business process preferred. <li>Cloud Identity experience preferred. <li>SC-300 Microsoft Certified Identity and Access Administrator Associate preferred. <li>CISSP Certified Information Systems Security Professional preferred. </ul> \]\]>

backups, recovery operations, and system maintenance. <li>Develop mappings, mapplets, sessions, and workflows using a wide range of Informatica transformations. <li>Monitor and troubleshoot ETL jobs across development, testing, and production environments. <li>Write and optimize complex SQL queries and Unix Shell scripts for data marts and interfaces in Teradata. <li>Collaborate with stakeholders <description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Overview & Role Focus</strong></p> <p>This role is centered on innovating and advancing state-of-the-art video processing and transport capabilities, delivering high-performance solutions on some of the most integrated poadcast hardware platforms available today. The successful candidate will work hands-on with FPGA design, real-time media interfaces, and poadcast protocol implementation, playing a key role across architecture, development, testing, and cross-functional support.</p> <p><strong>Key Responsibilities</strong></p> <ul> <li>Lead the development and continuous improvement of advanced video transport and processing features within tightly integrated poadcast hardware. <li>Design RTL for real-time, high-throughput media systems involving advanced interfaces—such as PCIe, memory, and specialized hardware acceleration (e.g., video scaling, HDR/SDR conversion). <li>Implement FPGA-based real-time transport protocols like SMPTE 2110 and SDI. <li>Participate in architectural planning: advise on FPGA density, schematic reviews, clocking strategies, and thermal considerations. <li>Build complete IO ring designs across modern FPGAs (Arria10, Stratix-10, Ultrascale+, MPSoC, Agilex) and validate pin-outs/IP within Quartus and Vivado environments. <li>Define and negotiate high-level design specs, assist in part selection, and align with aggressive project timelines. <li>Contribute to design specifications and documentation used by cross-functional teams. <li>Collaborate closely with peers on design verification and testing of FPGA and hardware systems. <li>Tackle debugging with a methodical and efficient approach. <li>Support team members throughout the entire New Product Introduction (NPI) lifecycle—from design through manufacturing to customer support. </ul> <p><strong>Required Skills & Background</strong></p> <ul> <li>5+ years in FPGA and hardware development, with a strong preference for experience in video/audio-centric technologies. <li>Intermediate to senior-level expertise in FPGA architecture and core components. <li>Deep understanding of high-speed serial interfaces, clock domains, timing closure, and transceiver integration. <li>Proficiency in Verilog, SystemVerilog, and TCL scripting; capable of creating testbenches and running simulations (e.g., VCS). <li>Familiarity with modern Intel and Xilinx FPGA families and their development/debugging toolchains. <li>Hands-on experience with interfaces like DDR3/DDR4, HBM, PLLs, and gigabit transceivers. <li>Skilled in lab-based debugging using oscilloscopes, JBERTs, network analyzers, waveform monitors, etc. <li>Embedded system awareness—experience with Linux, C/C++, bash scripting, and networking considered valuable. <li>Broadcast studio domain knowledge is highly desirable, especially within video production and distribution workflows. <li>A strong grasp of digital video/audio standards and signal integrity is considered a plus. <li>Driven and independent, yet collaborative—equally adept at working solo or influencing poader team strategies. <li>Quick learner with a creative mindset and ability to push ideas from concept to market. <li>Comfortable making bold decisions that balance quality, speed, and cost for optimal business outcomes. <li>Effective communicator with sharp observational skills and a problem-solving mindset. </ul> \]\]>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Job Title: Senior Identity and Access Management (IAM) Consultant – Oracle 12C OIM Data Migration</strong></p> <p><strong>Background:</strong></p> <p>Ontario Health’s <strong>ONE ID</strong> service is a secure identity management solution utilized by the Ministry of Health and Long-Term Care, as well as numerous healthcare organizations across Ontario. It enables secure access to patient health information (PHI) through a single set of login credentials while upholding stringent privacy and security standards.</p> <p>The ONE ID platform is based on the Oracle Identity and Access Management suite, including Oracle Access Manager (OAM), Oracle Unified Directory (OUD), Oracle Identity Manager (OIM), Oracle Database, Microsoft Active Directory (AD), and custom Ontario Health systems.</p> <p>Ontario Health is undertaking an upgrade to Oracle 12C IAM and requires the services of a <strong>Senior Identity and Access Management Consultant</strong> to support the data migration and integration activities necessary to transition from Oracle 10G/11G to 12C. The consultant will be embedded within a dedicated project team responsible for the 12C Oracle IAM upgrade.</p> <hr> <h3><strong>Must-Have Qualifications:</strong></h3> <ul> <li> <p>Minimum 7 years of experience as a Solution Architect on Oracle Identity and Access Management systems (10G, 11G, 12C).</p> <li> <p>Minimum 7 years of experience with 12C Oracle Identity Governance (OIG), including successful migration of user, service enrollment, and organizational data from 10G to 12C.</p> <li> <p>Minimum 5 years of experience configuring 11G OIM and 12C OIG in a multi-data center (MDC) environment.</p> <li> <p>Minimum 7 years of experience integrating Oracle IAM suite components: OAM, OIM, OUD/OVD, Oracle HTTP Server (OHS), Microsoft Active Directory, and Oracle databases.</p> <li> <p>Minimum 5 years of experience tuning Oracle IAM for high availability on WebLogic and Linux platforms.</p> <li> <p>Experience designing and creating services and applications for enrollment in 12C OIG using native interfaces.</p> <li> <p>Experience configuring connectors and disconnected resources for service/application enrollment in 12C OIG.</p> <li> <p>Must be associated with a recognized Gold Oracle IAM Partner.</p> <li> <p>Expertise in SAML 2.0 and OAuth 2.0 protocols.</p> <li> <p>Proven ability to translate conceptual, logical, and physical application architectures aligned to business and technical goals.</p> <li> <p>Strong written and verbal communication skills with the ability to clearly articulate technical issues and propose viable solutions.</p> <li> <p>Ability to produce comprehensive technical documentation including design, deployment, and integration guides.</p> </ul> <hr> <h3><strong>Responsibilities:</strong></h3> <ul> <li> <p>Collaborate with Ontario Health teams to design and configure 12C OIG in a multi-data center setup for both lower and upper environments.</p> <li> <p>Integrate Phase 1 of 12C MDC with the existing 10G ONE ID system to enable interoperability for user and service transition.</p> <li> <p>Create and maintain service/application enrollments in 12C OIG.</p> <li> <p>Develop enrollment flows for individual services/applications.</p> <li> <p>Document design, installation, configuration, and integration procedures across all environments.</p> <li> <p>Collaborate with the Applications and Architecture clinical workflows.</p> <p><strong>Key Responsibilities:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Support ambulatory care design and configuration initiatives.</p> <li> <p>Facilitate strategy execution and knowledge <description>

<!\[CDATA\[ As a RF Systems Engineer, you’ll be responsible for simulating and modeling the terrestrial and in-orbit communication systems for Lightspeed and support the definition of the architecture. <h2>Main Responsibilities</h2> <ul> <li>Simulate and model communication systems <li>Work with system architects, RF engineers, antenna engineers, User Terminal and Landing Station engineers, to partition functions between hardware and software domains <li>Model RF link performance and manage link budgets accounting for impairments through the different elements in the system <li>Derive specifications for RF links and RF and antenna subsystems <li>Characterize and analyze system performance. Develop and maintain performance budgets <li>Provide technical support to regulatory, coordination, and market access teams </ul> <h2>Education & Experience Required</h2> <ul> <li>Bachelor's degree in electrical engineering with emphasis in RF/microwave circuits or communication theory <li>At least 5 years of relevant experience RF communication systems <li>Knowledge of digital communication systems, spread spectrum, single and multi-carrier techniques, modulation types such as PSK, APSK, QAM <li>Specific experience with modulation standard such as DVB-S2X and DVB-RCS2, as well as with Adaptive Coding and Modulation (ACM) methods <li>Good experience in MATLAB or other tools for modeling and analyzing RF communication systems </ul> <h2>Specialized Knowledge, Skills & Abilities</h2> <ul> <li>Experience performing analysis and simulation of communication systems <li>Thorough understanding of RF passive and active components <li>Good understanding of active antenna beam forming technologies including digital beam forming, and fast beam hopping <li>Experience characterizing radio performance at microwave frequencies, including rain fade and its effects on the communication links <li>Knowledge of RF transceiver architectures and digital communication theor </ul> \]\]>

<!\[CDATA\[ Senior Manager, Radio System Engineering (32647) \]\]>

...

</title>

<company>

<!\[CDATA\[ Myticas Consulting \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>As the Senior Manager of Radio System Engineering, you will lead all technical aspects of radio system architecture, including air interface definition, concept of operations, functional specifications, and physical implementation of RF functions.</p> <hr> <p><strong>Main Responsibilities:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Provide expert-level leadership in RF system development, including trade-offs involving ACP, PAR, out-of-band emissions, pass-band ripple, group delay, and more.</p> <li> <p>Support the finalization of radio system implementation involving agile multi-beam phased array antennas and beam hopping technology.</p> <li> <p>Define operational concepts for all phases of the system lifecycle such as user terminal commissioning, network entry, satellite handovers, time synchronization, and adaptive coding and modulation (ACM).</p> <li> <p>Act as the principal architect for defining air interfaces between user terminals, ground infrastructure, and satellite payloads.</p> <li> <p>Collaborate with RF, antenna, system, and terminal engineers to partition functionality between hardware and software components.</p> <li> <p>Provide input to the system modeling team on design assumptions and strategies for modeling link performance, accounting for impairments across system components.</p> <li> <p>Work closely with the Verification and Test team to ensure thorough validation of requirements and system performance.</p> <li> <p>Participate in relevant industry standards forums (e.g., DVB) and provide strategic recommendations to align internal systems with evolving standards.</p> </ul> <hr> <p><strong>Education & Experience – Required:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Bachelor’s degree in Electrical, Computer, or Systems Engineering.</p> <li> <p>15+ years of experience in RF communications systems and/or RF equipment development.</p> <li> <p>Demonstrated experience taking RF systems from concept through iterative design, specification development, and low-rate production.</p> <li> <p>Strong background in system architecture, requirements management, and performance assessment for communication systems.</p> </ul> <hr> <p><strong>Education & Experience – Assets:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Familiarity with DVB standards such as DVB-S2X and DVB-RCS2.</p> <li> <p>Solid understanding of digital communications, spread spectrum techniques, single and multi-carrier modulation (e.g., PSK, APSK, QAM).</p> <li> <p>Proficiency in MATLAB or equivalent tools for modeling and analyzing RF communication systems.</p> <li> <p>Deep knowledge of RF passive and active components and microwave frequency performance, including the effects of environmental factors such as rain fade.</p> <li> <p>Strong foundation in RF transceiver architecture and digital communication theory.</p> <li> <p>Excellent communication skills, with the ability to effectively engage stakeholders across engineering, management, and external partners.</p> <li> <p>Collaborative, adaptable, and capable of leading multidisciplinary teams in high-performance environments.</p> </ul> \]\]>

...

</description>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Main Responsibilities:</strong></p> <p><strong>Configuration Identification</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Support and coordinate activities to establish rules for configuration item (CI) selection and baseline content definition.</p> <li> <p>Assist in selecting configuration items at appropriate levels of the product structure, including determining required configuration documentation for each CI.</p> </ul> <p><strong>Asset and Physical Systems Configuration Management</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Define, develop, and manage processes, procedures, and tools to identify, document, and control physical assets for a large-scale communications system.</p> <li> <p>Provide support for export control compliance processes such as ITAR.</p> <li> <p>Maintain an inventory of system assets (hardware).</p> <li> <p>Control and document system, hardware, and software configurations, including both "as-designed" and "as-built" baselines.</p> </ul> <p><strong>Software Configuration Management – Release Monitoring</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Collaborate with technical teams and project management to define roles and responsibilities for configuration and release management.</p> <li> <p>Work with development, test environment, and verification teams to define and document processes for managing software releases.</p> <li> <p>For each release, verify required documentation is complete, approved, and captured, and ensure release packages are created in accordance with established procedures.</p> <li> <p>Confirm that pending or outstanding changes do not impact planned test or release activities.</p> <li> <p>Support development, lab, and test teams to ensure timely and accurate release execution.</p> <li> <p>Assist with impact assessments and update the CI Tree and related configuration documentation to reflect approved changes.</p> <li> <p>Support preparation and execution of configuration item status accounting and configuration audits.</p> <li> <p>Provide subject matter expertise on configuration management (CM) processes, standards, and systems.</p> <li> <p>Contribute to requirements management and traceability process documentation and improvement.</p> <li> <p>Develop training materials for CM identification, software/release management, and general CM procedures.</p> <li> <p>Participate in continuous improvement initiatives to enhance CM process efficiency, reliability, and cost-effectiveness.</p> </ul> <p><strong>Document and Library Management Support</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Initiate updates to documentation based on approved change requests.</p> <li> <p>Collaborate with document management personnel to track and complete implementation of documentation updates.</p> <li> <p>Ensure all released documents are logged, captured, and statused in the document management system.</p> <li> <p>Act as backup support for document management responsibilities when needed.</p> </ul> <p><strong>Education & Experience – Required</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Bachelor’s or college degree in engineering, science, or a related field (or equivalent combination of education and experience).</p> <li> <p>3–6 years of experience in an engineering design environment working with systems, hardware, software, and test teams.</p> <li> <p>2+ years of experience in configuration and/or data management.</p> <li> <p>2+ years of experience in release management.</p> <li> <p>Formal training, certification, or experience with CM standards (e.g., CM2, ANSI-EIA 649, ISO 10007).</p> </ul> <p><strong>Education & Experience:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Experience with software configuration management tools and processes.</p> <li> <p>Strong verbal and written communication skills with both technical and non-technical audiences.</p> <li> <p>Experience in high-performing, multidisciplinary development teams.</p> <li> <p>Collaborative, team-oriented, and self-driven.</p> <li> <p>Skilled in Microsoft Office at an intermediate level.</p> <li> <p>Bilingual in English and French is an asset (but not required).</p> </ul> \]\]>
